 The festival of Makar Sankranti was celebrated with pomp across the country
 makar sankranti ugte suraj kaa parv he
 It is believed that the course of the seasons changes as the sun rises and the weather starts moving from winter to spring
 makar sankranti ke din surya uttarayan hota he or makar raashi main pravesh karata he
 At such a time, harmful rays come out of the sun, but there is no effect of rays in water, so it is the custom to bathe in rivers during Sankranti
 desh bhar ke log kareeb kii nadiyon main dubkee laga rahe hai
 In Haridwar, Allahabad and Varanasi, people have reached to dip in the Ganges on this occasion
 surya swasthya ke bhi devtaa hai
 Taking a bath in holy rivers on Makar Sankranti keeps the body free from diseases
 kehete hai makarsankranti ke din ganga nadi main snaan karne or daan punya karne se bhakton ko kai guna zyada fal miltaa he
 There is a tradition of donating white and black sesame on this occasion
